SWIG-wrapped TexGen C++ API entry for `or`.

#### `CDomain`

```cpp
class CLASS_DECLSPEC CDomain {
```

Abstract base class representing the domain in which a textile cell may lie

#### `~CDomain`

```cpp
virtual ~CDomain(void);
```

SWIG-wrapped TexGen C++ API entry for `~CDomain`.

#### `Copy`

```cpp
virtual CDomain* Copy() const = 0;
```

Return a copy of CDomain.

#### `PopulateTiXmlElement`

```cpp
virtual void PopulateTiXmlElement(TiXmlElement &Element, OUTPUT_TYPE OutputType = OUTPUT_STANDARD) const;
```

Used for saving data to XML

#### `GetRepeatLimits`

```cpp
vector<pair<int, int> > GetRepeatLimits(const CYarn &Yarn) const;
```

Get the limits associated with each repeat vector, that is the upper and lower bounds multiplied to
the repeat vector for the entire yarn to lie just outside out of the domain

#### `GetTranslations`

```cpp
vector<XYZ> GetTranslations(const CYarn &Yarn) const;
```

Get the translation vectors necessary to fully fill the domain

#### `ClipMeshToDomain`

```cpp
virtual void ClipMeshToDomain(CMesh &Mesh, bool bFillGaps = true) const = 0;
```

Clip the surface elements to the domain

For surface elements (TRI and QUAD elements) the elements will be either kept, discarded
or trimmed depending on their location relative to the domain.
For volume elements (TET, HEX) the elements will be either kept or discarded. No trimming
occurs in this case to avoid poorly shaped elements. The center of the element is used to
determine whether the element should be kept or discarded. For certain finite element analyses
simulations can be performed without any trimming.
param Mesh The mesh instance to be clipped, this will be modified in place
param bFillGaps If set to true the resulting holes will be filled with a triangulated mesh

#### `ClipMeshToDomain`

```cpp
virtual bool ClipMeshToDomain(CMesh &Mesh, vector<CMesh> &DomainMeshes, bool bFillGaps = true) const = 0;
```

Clip the surface elements to the domain

param Mesh The mesh instance to be clipped, this will be modified in place
param DomainMeshes One mesh for each plane which domain/mesh intersection polygons are added
param bFillGaps If set to true the resulting holes will be filled with a triangulated mesh

#### `GetType`

```cpp
virtual string GetType() const = 0;
```

Derived class should return the class name

#### `GetMesh`

```cpp
const CMesh &GetMesh() const { return m_Mesh; }
```

Get the mesh representing the domain as a surface mesh

#### `GetVolume`

```cpp
virtual double GetVolume() const;
```

Get the volume of the domain

#### `Grow`

```cpp
virtual void Grow(double dDistance) = 0;
```

Make the domain larger (used mainly for rendering purposes)

#### `Rotate`

```cpp
virtual void Rotate(WXYZ Rotation) = 0;
```

Rotate the domain by given rotation quaternion

#### `Translate`

```cpp
virtual void Translate(XYZ Vector) = 0;
```

Translate the domain by given vector

#### `Deform`

```cpp
virtual void Deform(CLinearTransformation Transformation) = 0;
```

Deform the domain by given linear transformation

#### `PointInDomain`

```cpp
virtual bool PointInDomain(const XYZ &Point) const = 0;
```

Check if a point lies inside the domain

#### `GetPrismDomain`

```cpp
CDomainPrism* GetPrismDomain();
```

Return prism domain from CDomain.

#### `ConvertLimitsToInt`

```cpp
static vector<pair<int, int> > ConvertLimitsToInt(const vector<pair<double, double> > &RepeatLimits);
```

Convert limits to int for CDomain.

#### `GetLimits`

```cpp
pair<double, double> GetLimits(XYZ RepeatVector, const CMesh &Mesh) const;
```

Get the limits for a single given repeat vector and surface mesh

The limits are the points where the whole surface mesh lies outside the domain
The limit is represented as the factor multiplied by the repeat vector that represents
the translation of the surface mesh to the limiting case.
param RepeatVector The repeat vector to get limit for
param Mesh The surface mesh that needs to lie behind the plane
return A pair of doubles representing the upper and lower limits

#### `MeshIntersectsDomain`

```cpp
bool MeshIntersectsDomain(const CMesh &Mesh) const;
```

Determine if a mesh intersects with the domain

This is a very crude approximation of whether a mesh intersects the domain or not.
It is based soley on the axis aligned bounding boxes of the two regions.

### `Core/DomainPlanes.h`

#### `or`

```cpp
of the License, or (at your option) any later version. This program is distributed in the hope that it will be useful, but WITHOUT ANY WARRANTY; without even the implied warranty of
```

SWIG-wrapped TexGen C++ API entry for `or`.

#### `CDomainPlanes`

```cpp
class CLASS_DECLSPEC CDomainPlanes : public CDomain {
```

Domain implementation described using planes, the simplest of which would be a box

The domain must describe an enclosed area in which the textile lies. If not enough planes are
specified the domain may be infinite, in which case bad things may happen.
A plane is described by a normal and a value that represents the shortest distance from the plane
to the origin (0, 0, 0). The normal should point towards the inside of the domain.

#### `Copy`

```cpp
CDomain* Copy() const { return new CDomainPlanes(*this); }
```

Return a copy of CDomainPlanes.

#### `PopulateTiXmlElement`

```cpp

```

Populate ti xml element from CDomainPlanes.

```cpp
void ClipMeshToDomain(CMesh &Mesh, bool bFillGaps = true) const;
```

SWIG-wrapped TexGen C++ API entry for `ClipMeshToDomain`.

```cpp

```

SWIG-wrapped TexGen C++ API entry for `ClipMeshToDomain`.



```cpp

```

Given a mesh and a plane, the holes found in the plane will be filled with triangles
Intersection of mesh and plane returned as closed loop

### `Core/DomainPrism.h`

#### `or`

```cpp
of the License, or (at your option) any later version. This program is distributed in the hope that it will be useful, but WITHOUT ANY WARRANTY; without even the implied warranty of
```

SWIG-wrapped TexGen C++ API entry for `or`.

#### `CDomainPrism`

```cpp
class CLASS_DECLSPEC CDomainPrism : public CDomain {
```

Domain implementation described using extrusion of a polygon outline

Prism is described by a yarn with two nodes (to give the orientation )
and a cross-section defined by a polygon section created using the vector of points given as an input parameter

#### `Copy`

```cpp
CDomain* Copy() const { return new CDomainPrism(*this); }
```

Return a copy of CDomainPrism.

#### `PopulateTiXmlElement`


Populate ti xml element from CDomainPrism.

#### `GetRepeatLimits`

```cpp
vector<pair<int, int> > GetRepeatLimits(const CYarn &Yarn) const { return vector<pair<int, int> >(); }
```

Get a vector of repeat limits for a given yarn. The number of limit pairs is the same
as the number of infinite repeats in the yarn.

#### `GetTranslations`

```cpp
vector<XYZ> GetTranslations(const CYarn &Yarn) const { return vector<XYZ>(); }
```

Get the translation vectors necessary to fully fill the domain

#### `ClipMeshToDomain`

```cpp
void ClipMeshToDomain(CMesh &Mesh, bool bFillGaps = true) const;
```

Clips a mesh passed to the function to the domain by using the PointInsideYarn function (for the domain 'yarn')
Creates intersection mesh of intersecting elements for further testing against each domain plane

#### `ClipIntersectMeshToDomain`


Checks each mesh element against each domain plane


#### `BuildMesh`

```cpp
void BuildMesh();
```

Get the limits for a single given repeat vector and surface mesh

The limits are the points where the whole surface mesh lies outside the domain
The limit is represented as the factor multiplied by the repeat vector that represents
the translation of the surface mesh to the limiting case.
param RepeatVector The repeat vector to get limit for
param Mesh The surface mesh that needs to lie behind the plane
return A pair of doubles representing the upper and lower limits

Determine if a mesh intersects with the domain

This is a very crude approximation of whether a mesh intersects the domain or not.
It is based soley on the axis aligned bounding boxes of the two regions.

Populate m_PlaneIntersections and m_Mesh, note this only works for closed domains

#### `GetPlane`

```cpp
bool GetPlane(XYZ *points, PLANE &plane);
```

Generate a plane from a vector of co-planar points

#### `RemoveDuplicatePlanes`

```cpp
void RemoveDuplicatePlanes();
```

Iterate through m_ElementPlanes to remove duplicates

#### `PlaneEqual`

```cpp
bool PlaneEqual(PLANE Plane1, PLANE Plane2);
```

Test if both normal and d of two PLANE structures are equal

#### `FillGaps`

```cpp
static bool FillGaps(CMesh &Mesh, const PLANE &Plane, vector<int> &Polygon, bool bMeshGaps = true);
```

Given a mesh and a plane, the holes found in the plane will be filled with triangles
Intersection of mesh and plane returned as closed loop

#### `CFibreDistribution`

```cpp
class CLASS_DECLSPEC CFibreDistribution {
```

Abstract base class that defines how the fibres are distributed within a yarn

This class is there to provide local volume fraction information for a yarn
cross section, from this different Vf distributions can be derived


#### `SaveVoxelMesh`

```cpp
virtual void SaveVoxelMesh(CTextile &Textile, string OutputFilename, int XVoxNum, int YVoxNum, int ZVoxNum, bool bOutputMatrix, bool bOutputYarns, int iBoundaryConditions, int iElementType = 0, int FileType = INP_EXPORT);
```

Save the voxel mesh as an Abaqus input file with periodic boundary conditions
param CTextile Textile - textile to be exported as refined voxel mesh
param string OutputFilename - filename to save to
param int XVoxNum - number of voxels in x direction
param int YVoxNum - number of voxels in y direction
param int ZVoxNum - number of voxels in z direction
param bOutputMatrix True to output the matrix area of the mesh
param bOutputYarns True to output the yarn areas
param iBoundaryConditions as in enum PERIODIC_BOUNDARY_CONDITIONS
param iElementType 0 for C3D8R, 1 for C3D8
param int Filetype as in enum EXPORT_TYPE

#### `AddElementInfo`


### `Core/TetgenMesh.h`

#### `or`

```cpp
of the License, or (at your option) any later version. This program is distributed in the hope that it will be useful, but WITHOUT ANY WARRANTY; without even the implied warranty of
```

SWIG-wrapped TexGen C++ API entry for `or`.

#### `CTetgenMesh`

```cpp
class CLASS_DECLSPEC CTetgenMesh : public CMeshDomainPlane {
```

Class which tetrahedralizes a textile using Tetgen software
The surface mesh and domain are used as tetgen input, the domain boundaries first being
triangulated such that opposite boundaries have the same input mesh. (This assumes that
the domain is specified to be a whole number of textile repeats).

#### `~CTetgenMesh`

```cpp
virtual ~CTetgenMesh(void);
```

SWIG-wrapped TexGen C++ API entry for `~CTetgenMesh`.

#### `SaveTetgenMesh`

```cpp
void SaveTetgenMesh(CTextile &Textile, string OutputFilename, string Parameters, bool bPeriodic, int FileType );
```

Save a textile as a tetrahedralized mesh using Tetgen

param Textile Textile to be meshed
param Filename for Tetgen output files
param Parameters tetgen flags to be applied during tetrahedralization
param bPeriodic If set true, opposite faces of mesh will be replicated

#### `SaveMesh`

```cpp
void SaveMesh(CTextile &Textile);
```

Save tetgenio data to CMesh

#### `SaveToAbaqus`

```cpp
void SaveToAbaqus( string Filename, CTextile &Textile );
```

Save output mesh to Abaqus export file

#### `SaveToVTK`

```cpp

```

#### `COctreeVoxelMesh`

```cpp
class CLASS_DECLSPEC COctreeVoxelMesh : public CVoxelMesh {
```

Class used to generate octree-refine voxel mesh for output to ABAQUS

#### `~COctreeVoxelMesh`

```cpp
virtual ~COctreeVoxelMesh(void);
```

SWIG-wrapped TexGen C++ API entry for `~COctreeVoxelMesh`.

#### `SaveVoxelMesh`

```cpp
void SaveVoxelMesh(CTextile &Textile, string OutputFilename, int XVoxNum, int YVoxNum, int ZVoxNum, int min_level, int refine_level, bool smoothing, int smoothIter, double smooth1, double smooth2, bool surfaceOuput);
```

Save Octree-refined mesh with an option of surface smoothing
param int min_level
param int refine_level - maximum refinement level
param bool smoothing True to enable surface smoothing
param int smoothIter to control number of smoothing iterations
param double smooth1 is the first smoothing parameter
param double smooth2 is the second smoothing parameter

SWIG-wrapped TexGen C++ API entry for `or`.

#### `CSurfaceMesh`

```cpp
class CLASS_DECLSPEC CSurfaceMesh : public CMeshDomainPlane {
```

Class which generates a surface mesh with triangulated domain boundaries
(This assumes that
the domain is specified to be a whole number of textile repeats).

#### `~CSurfaceMesh`

```cpp
virtual ~CSurfaceMesh(void);
```

SWIG-wrapped TexGen C++ API entry for `~CSurfaceMesh`.

#### `SaveSurfaceMesh`

```cpp
void SaveSurfaceMesh(CTextile &Textile, bool bSaveYarns = true, bool bSaveDomain = false, bool bTrimToDomain = true);
```

Save a textile as a surface mesh with triangulated domain faces

param Textile Textile to be meshed
param bSaveYarns True if yarn surfaces to be saved
param bSaveDomain True if domain surfaces to be saved
param bTrimToDomain True if yarns are to be trimmed to domain surfaces

#### `SaveToSTL`

```cpp
void SaveToSTL(string Filename, bool bBinary);
```

Save surface mesh data to STL file

param Filename Filename to save data to
param bBinary True to save as binary file, False to save as ASCII

#### `SaveToVTK`

```cpp
void SaveToVTK(string Filename);
```

Save surface mesh data to VTK file

#### `SaveToSCIRun`

```cpp
void SaveToSCIRun(string Filename);
```

Save surface mesh data to SCIRun format

#### `CPatternDraft`

```cpp
class CLASS_DECLSPEC CPatternDraft {
```

Class used to calculate a pattern draft from a weave pattern
Also used to set up 3D model from a weave pattern

#### `~CPatternDraft`

```cpp
virtual ~CPatternDraft(void);
```

SWIG-wrapped TexGen C++ API entry for `~CPatternDraft`.

#### `AddRow`

```cpp
void AddRow( string Row );
```

Add a row representing one weft insertion '1' indicates warp up, '0' warp down and '2' no yarn



#### `CreateHeddleDraft`

```cpp
bool CreateHeddleDraft();
```

Create heddle draft. Stored as vector of int

#### `CreateChainDraft`

```cpp
bool CreateChainDraft();
```

Chain draft calculated from weave pattern and heddle draft.  Stored as vector of bools
Width = number of heddles
Height = number of wefts
